 iske alaava gwalior, sagar, umariya, raisen, hoshangabad, khargon or rajgad main adhiktam taapmaana 45 degree rahaa

 monsoon ke kam rahane kaa anumaanamausam vibhaag ke anusaar kerala main is baar monsoon paanch din kii deree se chah june ko pahunchane kaa anumaan he

 iemdi ke anusaar aamtaur par mana jaataa he ki al-nino monsoon par apana asar daalati he, jiskaa asar barish ke mausam main jari rahegaa

 2017 main bhi yahaan modi magic nahin chal sakaa

 haalanki 90 ke dashak main jile par bhagava rang chadhaane kii koshish hui, lekin bijepi ko badi kamyaabi nahin mil saki

 muslim-yadav ke factor ke jariye hi sapa1996 se ab tak paanch baar jeet kaa paracham laharaa chuki he

 basapa ne is seat par muslim-dalit cambination ke jariye 4 baar jeet hasil kii thi

 azamgarh sansadeey seat muslim-yadav bahulmaani jaati he

 yadav-muslim kii hissedari kareeb 40 fisadi he

 isi kaa nateeja he ki azamgarh main sapa or basapa kaa dabadabaa kaayam he

 par azamgarh loksabhaa seat jeetne main kaamyaab nahin ho sake the

 ramakant tatkaaleen bijepi se hi saansad the

 Mulayam Singh retained the sp's dominance by winning this seat through the muslim-yadav factor
 2017 ke vidhansabha chunaav main upi ke har jile main bijepi kaa jaadu chalaa, lekin azamgarh main koi asar nahin dikhaa sakaa
 While BJP won 311 seats for the first time in its history, in Azamgarh, it had to be content with just one seat
 2017 ke vidhansabha chunaav azamgarh kii 10 vidhansabha siton main se keval ek seat bijepi ke arunakanth yadav jeet sake the, jo ramakant yadav ke putr hai

 During that time one must maintain myself and be committed because this profession has given me so much

 main jo kar rahaa hum, use main apana behtareen de saktaa hum

 The science of soil studies is called soil science
 bhartiya krishi anusandhan parishad ne bharat kii mitti ko 8 virgon main baanta he
 1
 jalodh mitti (eluvial soil)>yah mitti bharat ke lagbhag 22 fisadi kshetrafal par pai jaati he
 > It is the soil brought by rivers
 is mitti main potash kii bahulata hoti he, lekin nitrogen, phosphorus or humas kii kami hoti he
 > This soil is of 2 types: -1
 bangar (bangar)2
 Khadar (khadar)> The old alluvial soil is called Bangar and the new alluvial soil is called Khadar
 >jalodh mitti urvartaa ke drushtikon se kaaphi acchhee maani jaati he
 In this, crops like paddy, wheat, maize, oilseeds, pulses etc
 are grown
 2
 Black soil> It is formed due to the breakage of basalt rocks
 isamen aayran, chuunaa, aluminium jeevansh or magnesium kii bahulata hoti he
 > The black color of this soil is due to the presence of tetaniferous magnetite and germs (humus)
 > is mitti ko regur mitti ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he
 Black soil is most suitable for cotton cultivation, hence it is also called black cotton soil i
e
 black cotton soil
 > anya fasalon main genhu, jowar, bajra aadi ko ugaaya jaataa he
 3
 laal mitti (red soil)> iskaa nirmaan jal vaayu parivartan kii vajah se ravedaar or kayantarit shailon ke vighatan or viyojan se hota he hota he
 > This soil is rich in silica and iron
 > laal mitti kaa laal rang aayran oxide kii upasthiti ke kaaran hota he, lekin jalyojit rup main yah pili dikhaai detii he
 > It is soil of acidic nature
 isamen nitrogen, phosphorus or humas kii kami hoti he
 > This soil is found as a fertile wasteland
 > is mitti main kapaas, genhu, daalen or mote anaajon kii kheti kii jaati he
 > In India, this soil is located in the eastern part of Andhra Pradesh and Madhya Pradesh, the plateau region of Chotanagpur, the northern west districts of West Bengal, the mountainous regions of Garo Khasi and Jaintia in Meghalaya, the eastern region of Aravali in Nagaland, Rajasthan, Maharashtra, Tamil Nadu and Karnataka
 It is found in some parts
 > chooney kaa istemaal kar laal mitti kii urvartaa badhaai ja sakati he
 4
 laterite mitti(laterite Soil)>iskaa nirmaan monsooni jalwaayu kii ardrata or shushkta ke kramik parivartan ke parinamswaroop utpann vishisht paristhitiyon main hota he
 > It contains a plurality of iron and silica
 >shailon yani rox kii tut-foot se nirmit hone vaali is mitti ko gahari laal laterite, safed laterite or bhumigat jalwaayi laterite ke rup main vargeekrut kiya jaataa he:> gahari laal lateritaisamen aayran oxide or potash kii bahulata hoti he
 Its fertility is low but some cultivation can be done in the lower part> White Latterite
 Its fertility is the lowest and due to kaolin its color is white
 > bhumigat jalwaayi lateraitayah mitti kaaphi upjau hoti he kyunki varshakaal main aayran oxide pani ke saath ghul kar neeche chale jate hai> laterite mitti chaay kii kheti ke liye sabase upyukt hoti he
